<script src="https://lamyrecipes.com/wp-includes/js/jquery/jquery.min.js?ver=3.7.1" id="jquery-core-js"></script>
<script src="https://lamyrecipes.com/wp-includes/js/jquery/jquery-migrate.min.js?ver=3.4.1" id="jquery-migrate-js"></script>
<script id="jquery-js-after">
jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
                    // PDF Download functionality - INSTANT DOWNLOAD via iframe
                    $(".recipe-pdf-download-button").on("click", function(e) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        var postId = $(this).data("post-id");
                        var resultDiv = $("#recipe-pdf-download-result");
                        var button = $(this);
                        
                        // Disable button and show loading state
                        button.prop("disabled", true);
                        button.css("opacity", "0.7");
                        resultDiv.html("<p class='pdf-generating'><span class='dashicons dashicons-update spin' style='margin-right:8px; animation: spin 2s linear infinite;'></span> Preparing your recipe card...</p>");
                        
                        $("<style>@keyframes spin { 0% { transform: rotate(0deg); } 100% { transform: rotate(360deg); } }</style>").appendTo("head");
                        
                        $.ajax({
                            url: "https://lamyrecipes.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php",
                            type: "POST",
                            data: {
                                action: "rw_generate_recipe_pdf",
                                post_id: postId,
                                nonce: "7fd17fc1fa"
                            },
                            success: function(response) {
                                if (response.success) {
                                    // INSTANT DOWNLOAD - Use download URL with proper headers
                                    var downloadUrl = "https://lamyrecipes.com/?rw_download_pdf=1&file=" + encodeURIComponent(response.data.pdf_file) + "&nonce=043dbdfd80";
                                    
                                    // Create hidden iframe to trigger download without opening new tab
                                    var iframe = document.createElement("iframe");
                                    iframe.style.display = "none";
                                    iframe.src = downloadUrl;
                                    document.body.appendChild(iframe);
                                    
                                    // Remove iframe after download starts
                                    setTimeout(function() {
                                        document.body.removeChild(iframe);
                                    }, 2000);
                                    
                                    // Show success message
                                    resultDiv.html("<p class='pdf-success'><span class='dashicons dashicons-yes-alt' style='margin-right:8px; color:#4CAF50;'></span> Download started! Check your downloads folder.</p>");
                                    
                                    // Re-enable button after short delay
                                    setTimeout(function() {
                                        button.prop("disabled", false);
                                        button.css("opacity", "1");
                                        resultDiv.html("");
                                    }, 3000);
                                } else {
                                    button.prop("disabled", false);
                                    button.css("opacity", "1");
                                    resultDiv.html("<p class='pdf-error'><span class='dashicons dashicons-warning' style='margin-right:8px;'></span> Error: " + response.data.message + "</p>");
                                }
                            },
                            error: function(xhr, status, error) {
                                button.prop("disabled", false);
                                button.css("opacity", "1");
                                var errorMsg = "Error generating PDF. Please try again.";
                                if (xhr.responseJSON && xhr.responseJSON.data && xhr.responseJSON.data.message) {
                                    errorMsg = xhr.responseJSON.data.message;
                                }
                                resultDiv.html("<p class='pdf-error'><span class='dashicons dashicons-warning' style='margin-right:8px;'></span> " + errorMsg + "</p>");
                            }
                        });
                    });
                    
                    // FAQ Accordion functionality
                    if ($(".rw-faq-item").length > 0) {
                        var accentColor = $(".rw-faq-container").data("accent-color") || "#FF6B6B";
                        
                        $(".rw-faq-item").on("click", function(e) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            var $item = $(this);
                            var $answer = $item.find(".rw-faq-answer");
                            var $toggle = $item.find(".rw-faq-toggle");
                            var isOpen = $item.hasClass("active");
                            
                            if (isOpen) {
                                $item.removeClass("active");
                                $answer.slideUp(400);
                                $toggle.text("+");
                            } else {
                                $(".rw-faq-item").removeClass("active");
                                $(".rw-faq-answer").slideUp(400);
                                $(".rw-faq-toggle").text("+");
                                
                                $item.addClass("active");
                                $answer.slideDown(400);
                                $toggle.text("−");
                            }
                        });
                    }
                });
            
//# sourceURL=jquery-js-after
</script>

<h2 class="kt-adv-heading4641_560237-25 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading4641_560237-25">Meet Evelyn &mdash; The Heart Behind Lamy Recipes</h2>



<p class="has-large-font-size">Hi, I&rsquo;m Evelyn! I believe that every dish has a story. Through Lamy Recipes, I share comforting meals inspired by family traditions and simple everyday joys. My goal is to bring warmth, flavor, and connection back to your kitchen.</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-advancedbtn kb-buttons-wrap kb-btns4641_43d6cc-d2"><a class="kb-button kt-button button kb-btn4641_0ee29e-2a kt-btn-size-large kt-btn-width-type-auto kb-btn-global-inherit  kt-btn-has-text-true kt-btn-has-svg-false  wp-block-button__link wp-block-kadence-singlebtn" href="https://lamyrecipes.com/about/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span class="kt-btn-inner-text">About me</span></a></div>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column4641_92b1d6-11"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column4641_3f83dd-b2 inner-column-1"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h1 class="kt-adv-heading4641_0e4b25-95 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading4641_0e4b25-95">The People Who Bring Warmth to Every Recipe</h1>



<p class="kt-adv-heading4641_1e7d7b-6c wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading4641_1e7d7b-6c">Behind every comforting meal at Lamy Recipes is a small team that believes food is more than taste &mdash; it&rsquo;s about memories, love, and connection. Meet the people who make it happen every day.</p>


<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id4641_26bdaa-c4 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kb-theme-content-width">
